  992. A great dupe for beauty blenders. The price is amazing for all the sponges you get. They are a bit stiff at first. I suggest you soak them in warm water with makeup brush cleaner for 20 minutes. Wring/squeeze them out and let them dry on the counter top. They do increase in size but not by much after wetting them. After drying, the sponges shrink down a bit, but not to their initial size.<br /><br />If applying wet or oil based products, dampen sponge with water first. This helps with application of products. It will seem like it is taking on a lot of product, but by wetting the sponge the water inside makes a weighted core which keeps most of the wet product your using on the outside of the sponge. Can also be used with dry/powdered products. You can use the same wetting process as oil based products but coverage will be heaver. My personal suggestion is to keep one of the sponges dry when setting makeup concealer under the eye.<br /><br />When dirty with product, wet them with water and take a dime size of makeup brush cleaner and another dime size of olive oil in your hand. Work these two products into the sponge. You will see the makeup starting to lift. After 30 seconds or so, continue to work the mixture into the sponge while under running warm water. In two minutes all the product should be lifted and you should have a clean sponge. A great buy. I would highly recommend you give them a try.

  1047. First off these are super cute! The colors and shapes are adorable (the colors of mine match the picture exactly). They did take a VERY long time to get here, but they do ship from either China or Korea. If you are an impatient person do not get these, instead buy the Real Techniques sponge. Even though these took a long time to arrive I still love them. At first they are rather hard and not very spongy, but the more I washed them, used them, and played around with them, the squishier they got. They are now soft and easy to use. Both shapes are great and work well. They apply makeup perfectly. However, with all beauty blender dupes, you have to use them and care for them properly or they will not work as well! To use you have to soak them in water and then squeeze out all the water you can, using a towel can help squeeze out the last bit of water (do not twist them to wring out water, that ruins them), and then use a foundation or concealer the is not watery because the sponge will soak up a watery foundation or a tinted moisturizer depositing less product on your face. You can still use these types of products, but they will not work as well. To clean them, squeeze water through them and apply either a facial cleanser that can remove makeup, dish soap, or a special beauty blender sponge cleaner, the bar version is supposed to work better than the liquid one. Be sure to thoroughly rinse with water, squeezing to get all of the makeup out, until the water runs clear. Wash after each use and allow to air dry. Do not place in a container or wrap in a towel when allowing the sponge to dry. Some foundations and concealers will stain the sponges, just wash the areas used for applying makeup with soap to insure that they are completely clean. If you take good care of your sponges, then they should last a long time no matter where they were bought. I love these sponges and am very happy that I bought them!
